    FROM [CartLogDetail] AS [c1]
    INNER JOIN [Linen] AS [l0] ON [c1].[LinenId] = [l0].[LinenId]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[CartLogId] = [t0].[CartLogId]
ORDER BY [t].[CartLogId], [t].[CartId0], [t].[EmployeeId0], [t].[LocationId0], [t0].[CartLogDetailId]
